from openapi_client.rest import ApiException
from pprint import pprint

# Defining the host is optional and defaults to https://demo.netbox.dev/api
# See configuration.py for a list of all supported configuration parameters.
configuration = openapi_client.Configuration(
    host = "https://demo.netbox.dev/api"
)

# The client must configure the authentication and authorization parameters
# in accordance with the API server security policy.
# Examples for each auth method are provided below, use the example that
# satisfies your auth use case.

# Configure API key authorization: Bearer
configuration.api_key['Bearer'] = os.environ["API_KEY"]

# Uncomment below to setup prefix (e.g. Bearer) for API key, if needed
# configuration.api_key_prefix['Bearer'] = 'Bearer'

# Enter a context with an instance of the API client
with openapi_client.ApiClient(configuration) as api_client:
    # Create an instance of the API class
    api_instance = openapi_client.IpamApi(api_client)

    try:
        api_instance.ipam_aggregates_bulk_delete()
    except Exception as e:
        print("Exception when calling IpamApi->ipam_aggregates_bulk_delete: %s\n" % e)
